            <div class="col-xs-12 col-md-9">
                <h1>
                    Mouse Playhouse
                </h1>
                
                <div class="studio-information">
                    <span>Cohort
                        25
                        |</span>
                    <span>
                        Tinkertainment
                        :</span>
                    <span>
                        Clay Howell, Taylor Bishop, Ben Gibson, Jeremy Hicks, Komal Kanukuntla, Michael Feffer, Alexandre Foures, Steve Kocher, Jacob Lavender, James Lee, Sam Pate, Taylor McCart, Devanshu Bishnoi, Nina Davis, Taylor Gallagher, Mace Mulleady, Mitchell Massey, Mario Rodriguez
                    </span>
                </div>
                

                <div class="row body">
                    <div class="col-xs-12">
                        <div class="dark-background"></div>
                        <div class="col-xs-12 col-sm-6 image ">
                            <img src="/-/media/Site/Guildhall/images/team-game-projects/MousePlayhouse_Poster_web.jpg?h=360&amp;iar=0&amp;w=280&amp;hash=059797698D1039222B1508706594C00E" class="box-shadow" alt="placeholder-280x360" width="280" height="360">
                        </div>
                        <div class="col-xs-12 col-sm-6 content ">

                            <p><em>Mouse Playhouse</em> is a light-hearted VR puzzle game in which you manipulate objects to solve puzzles and guide your pet mice towards the cheese. </p>
<p>In <em>Mouse Playhouse</em>, you can also throw objects around and play basketball, darts and even the xylophone. There are a total of 15 levels and each one presents a unique challenge. Players must use the blue objects provided to guide the mice away from trouble and towards the cheese.</p>
<br>


                            <div>
                                <a href="https://youtu.be/_BCBCv1to7M" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="red-button" target="_blank">
                                    YouTube
                                </a>
                            </div>

                            <div>
                                <a href="https://store.steampowered.com/app/612590/Mouse_Playhouse/?curator_clanid=34088398" class="red-button">
                                    Download
                                </a>
                            </div>

                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>

                                <div class="row">
                                    <div class="modal-summary col-xs-12">
                                        <p>A.N.D.Y. is a 2D platformer game in which players play as Zu_An, a time traveler trapped in the 14th century with a high-tech suit powered by an Artificial Neutron Displacement Yield (A.N.D.Y.) capable of warping through time and creating an energy shield. After crashing from his time warp into a medieval fortress, Zu_An must explore the fortress by running and jumping across platforms while collecting all four missing pieces of A.N.D.Y. In addition, Zu_An deploys his energy shield to catch projectiles and redirect them as a weapon or as a tool to trigger levers to open gates.<br>
<br>
ANDY was developed by Cohort 25 team Literally ANDY as part of the Team Game Production 1 class and was one of the very first games developed by Cohort 25.</p>

                                <div class="row">
                                    <div class="modal-summary col-xs-12">
                                        <p><span><em>Doctors Note </em>is a 2D puzzle game for tablet and mobile devices. Players take the role of a mad scientist placing gears on pegs to rotate and move pipes into place, ultimately leading to the creation of the doctors Frankenstein-esque monster. Players interact with the puzzles by placing gears from their tray onto pegs in individual puzzles, which results in pipes moving into place and triggering the activation of other pegs and objects. Players only get a general sense for the vibe of the game and what theyre actually creating, and only realize at the end what they were building through each of the five puzzles.</span></p>
<p>
<br>
<em>Doctor's Note</em> was developed by Cohort 25 team It's Alive Studios as part of the Team Game Production 1 class and was one of the very first games developed by Cohort 25.</p>

                                <div class="row">
                                    <div class="modal-summary col-xs-12">
                                        <p><em>For the Family</em> is a multiplayer first-person shooter (FPS) capture-the-flag (CTF) game set in Prohibition-era Chicago. Players take the role of mafia enforcers fighting for control of the illegal alcohol trade, but not without indulging in a bit of drink themselves. Players regain health with every shot and swig from the bottle and race through the streets fueled with a generous dose of White Lightning moonshine. Players that take one too many swigs from the bottle also fly into a death-dealing Drunken Rage.</p>
<p>As mafia enforcers, players storm the streets of Chicago armed with iconic weapons of the time period: the 1911 semi-automatic pistol, the Winchester Model 12 Shotgun, and the Thompson Machine Gun, famously known as the Tommy Gun. The Tommy Gun features a fully-automatic primary fire mode and a more accurate single-shot secondary fire while the Shotgun boasts a hard-hitting shell spread for its primary fire and an explosive grenade launcher as its secondary.</p>
<p>For the Family features two maps: Bootlegger, in which Rosso and Azzurro families compete to steal the most liquor from the Lucky Clover jazz club, and Vendetta, where the Rosso and Azzurro families strive to steal each others precious flasks.</p>
<p><em><em><em><em>For the Family</em>&nbsp;</em></em></em>is a 3D game that was developed by Cohort 25 team Bullpup Games and was one of the first 3D games developed by Cohort 25. <em><em>&nbsp;</em></em></p>

Each teams sole objective is to bring the opponents flag back to their base while breaking through the opponents defense.&nbsp;</span>The game contains two levels, where the first level is a vanilla Capture-the-Flag (CTF) map and the second one is a special game mode we call: Flag-all-Out.</p>
<p><em><em><em><em><em>Iron Games</em></em>&nbsp;</em></em></em>is a 3D game that was developed by Cohort 25 team Moonblast Squadron and was one of the first 3D games developed by Cohort 25. <em><em>&nbsp;</em></em></p>

                                <div class="row">
                                    <div class="modal-information col-xs-12">

                                <div class="row">
                                    <div class="modal-summary col-xs-12">
                                        <p><span><em>King Pufferfish</em> is a </span><span>single player, third-person, endless, top-down, defensive shooter</span><span> game for Android tablets. The player controls the stationary Pufferfish avatar and shoots waves of invading enemies to protect a robust wall that represents his kingdoms border. The goal of the game is to prevent enemy sea creatures from reaching the wall by shooting them with the pufferfishs spines. The Players finger taps control shooting whereas swipes clear the screen of ink. Tapping on any location empowers King Pufferfish to shoot a spine in that direction. If aimed to collide with an enemy, the enemy flees the screen and dispels vision-blocking ink onto the screen. If the shot collides with an underwater mine, the player and the enemies take damage. Aiming is important, and rewards high accuracy with a score multiplier. Scrubbing the ink cleans it off the screen to restore visibility. Every fourth wave is a rage wave, where hordes of enemies bombard the player. To combat the horde, King Pufferfish enrages and fires rapidly with a swipe of the players finger. Although failure is inevitable, players leave with a high score to show off their expertise to their friends.</span></p>
<p><span><em> </em></span>
<br>
<em><em>King Pufferfish</em></em> was developed by Cohort 25 team Poseidon Entertainment as part of the Team Game Production 1 class and was one of the very first games developed by Cohort 25.</p>

                                <div class="row">
                                    <div class="modal-summary col-xs-12">
                                        <p><em><em>Kirie</em></em>&nbsp;is a 2D game that was developed by Cohort 25 team 2Face Entertainment as part of the Team Game Production 1 class and was one of the very first games developed by Cohort 25.&nbsp; </p>
<p>2Face Entertainment set out to create a unique gameplay experience that could only be accomplished within the medium of a tablet. After discussing various mechanics, the team gravitated toward the idea of cutting paper using a swiping motion. The team then used the core concept behind the mechanic to create a world inspired by origami and far-eastern culture.&nbsp;</p>

                                <div class="row">
                                    <div class="modal-summary col-xs-12">
                                        <p><em>Laika</em> is a top-down, vertical scrolling space adventure game in which players guide Laika, the Canine Cosmonaut, through treacherous obstacles and devious enemies. Set in an alternate past, <em>Laika </em>gives players the opportunity to rewrite the early history of the Space Race by guiding the titular heros Sputnik II rocket out of Earths orbit and into the solar system. </p>
<p>This mission decides the fate of the Soviet space program, which teeters on the brink of financial ruin after several failed launches of its radically advanced rocket technology. As she travels through space, Laika must collect funds and claim territories for the motherland. In the dark and dangerous depths of outer space, players must be vigilant to protect Laika from floating debris, asteroids, and hostile aliens.</p>
<p>Designed to be a lighthearted interpretation of a rather serious period in modern history, the visuals of <em>Laika</em> adopt a slightly cartoonish tone inspired by the propaganda prevalent during the Cold War/Space Race era. The games soundtrack features variations of the State Anthem of the Russian Federation.</p>
<p><em><em>Laika</em></em>&nbsp;is a 2D game that was developed by Cohort 25 team ALT 236 as part of the Team Game Production 1 class and was one of the very first games developed by Cohort 25. &nbsp;</p>

                                    <div class="modal-summary col-xs-12">
                                        <p><em>Lonely HAL</em>&nbsp;is an industrial-themed 2D puzzle game on Android. The protagonist character, HAL, is a helpless robot incapable of moving on his own. Players interact with environmental objects scattered throughout a factory to navigate HAL through a handful of treacherous levels and help him escape the factory to find his friend PAL.</p>
<p><em><em><em>Lonely HAL</em></em></em>&nbsp;is a 2D game that was developed by Cohort 25 team Mech Squad as part of the Team Game Production 1 class and was one of the very first games developed by Cohort 25. &nbsp;</p>

                        <div class="col-xs-6 col-sm-4 grid-listing" data-details="6E58238B53D9441F81965EB4247800B8" data-visible="False">
                            
                            <a class="link" href="javascript:;">
                                <img src="/-/media/Site/Guildhall/images/team-game-projects/REPulsePoster-web.jpg?h=360&amp;iar=0&amp;w=280&amp;hash=772556CDC2EAD0D3633B377444471500" alt="placeholder-280x360" width="280" height="360">
                                <div class="details">
                                    <div class="overlay"></div>
                                    <div class="sub-heading">
                                        Cohort
                                            25
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="name">
                                        RE.Pulse
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="view-details">
                                        View Details
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                            </a>
                        </div>
                        <div class="grid-listing-details-container" id="6E58238B53D9441F81965EB4247800B8">
                            <div class="grid-listing-details">
                                <div class="x" data-details="6E58238B53D9441F81965EB4247800B8">x</div>

                                <div class="row">
                                    <div class="name col-xs-12">
                                        RE.Pulse
                                    </div>
                                </div>

                                <div class="row">
                                    <div class="modal-information col-xs-12">
                                        <span>
                                            2D Game
                                            |</span>
                                        <span>
                                            Self-Propelled Studios
                                        </span>
                                    </div>
                                </div>

                                <div class="row">
                                    <div class="modal-summary col-xs-12">
                                        <p><span style="color: #333333; background: white;"><em>RE.Pulse</em>&nbsp;is a 2D Side-Scrolling puzzle game, taking place in a crystal infested nether void. The player takes control of Vasc, an interstellar traveler attempting to escape a mysterious, interdimensional&nbsp;void. To reach the exit, the player navigates Vasc through the world via a series of stationary and moving crystal cannons.&nbsp;The void is also infested with sharp, spikey crystal&nbsp;hazards.&nbsp;Vasc's suit is not puncture-resistant, so the player must&nbsp;carefully weave their way through&nbsp;the crystal fields in order for Vasc to survive the journey back.&nbsp;Utilizing a simple tap-to-shoot mechanic to move the player from cannon-to-cannon, RE.Pulse emphasizes a timing and reactionary style of gameplay.</span></p>
<p><em> <em><em><em style="color: #333333;">RE.Pulse</em></em></em></em>&nbsp;is a 2D game that was developed by Cohort 25 team Self-Propelled Studios as part of the Team Game Production 1 class and was one of the very first games developed by Cohort 25. &nbsp;</p>
                                    </div>
                                </div>

                                <div class="row">

                                    <div class="cols-xs-12 col-md-6  ">
                                        <a href="https://youtu.be/yeWtDVEiNc8" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="red-button" target="_blank">
                                            YouTube
                                        </a>
                                    </div>

                                    <div class="col-xs-12 col-md-6  ">
                                        <a class="red-button">
                                            Game Download
                                        </a>
                                    </div>

                                </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    
                        <div class="col-xs-6 col-sm-4 grid-listing" data-details="679BBC48225140928037131E7328D0BF" data-visible="False">
                            
                            <a class="link" href="javascript:;">
                                <img src="/-/media/Site/Guildhall/images/team-game-projects/BoomBoom_Poster-web.jpg?h=360&amp;iar=0&amp;w=280&amp;hash=9173DBBF8FADF721646D2D396AB5AB1E" alt="placeholder-280x360" width="280" height="360">
                                <div class="details">
                                    <div class="overlay"></div>
                                    <div class="sub-heading">
                                        Cohort
                                            25
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="name">
                                        The Adventures of Boom-Boom
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="view-details">
                                        View Details
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                            </a>
                        </div>
                        <div class="grid-listing-details-container" id="679BBC48225140928037131E7328D0BF">
                            <div class="grid-listing-details">
                                <div class="x" data-details="679BBC48225140928037131E7328D0BF">x</div>

                                <div class="row">
                                    <div class="name col-xs-12">
                                        The Adventures of Boom-Boom
                                    </div>
                                </div>

                                <div class="row">
                                    <div class="modal-information col-xs-12">
                                        <span>
                                            2D Game
                                            |</span>
                                        <span>
                                            Starfall
                                        </span>
                                    </div>
                                </div>

                                <div class="row">
                                    <div class="modal-summary col-xs-12">
                                        <p><em>The Adventures of Boom-Boom</em> is an explosive tablet game that challenges the players tilting and aiming skills. Players use the innovative accelerometer technology built into their tablets to defeat the obstacles in the steampunk universe of Gigaship City. The game follows Boom-Boom, the ten-year-old genius and illegitimate son of the rich corporate mogul Pa-Pa and a poor underground woman named Ma-Ma. After Pa-Pa starts replacing the workers of the underground city with his Gol-Gol workers, Ma-Ma threatens to go public with their love childs existence in attempt to give Boom-Boom a better life on the surface. However, Pa-Pa sends his Gol-Gols solders to silence her for good, leaving Boom-Boom with a destroyed home and hatred for Pa-Pa industries. Upon the death of his mother, Boom-Boom swears to take revenge by destroying all products of Pa-Pa industries with his steerable bombs and flying mech. The story presents players with an empathetic story that follows Boom-Booms feelings of revenge and justice via blowing up generators and Gol-Gols. The games explosive and immersive nature comes from the combination of its innovative artwork, mechanics, and story line. These immersive aesthetics give players a new and improved experience within the tablet gaming market place.&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
<p><em> <em><em><em>The Adventures of Boom-Boom</em></em></em></em>&nbsp;is a 2D game that was developed by Cohort 25 team Starfall as part of the Team Game Production 1 class and was one of the very first games developed by Cohort 25. &nbsp;</p>
                                    </div>
                                </div>

                                <div class="row">

                                    <div class="cols-xs-12 col-md-6  ">
                                        <a href="https://youtu.be/Lic3KFXiT9k" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="red-button" target="_blank">
                                            YouTube
                                        </a>
                                    </div>

                                    <div class="col-xs-12 col-md-6  ">
                                        <a class="red-button">
                                            Game Download
                                        </a>

                        <div class="col-xs-6 col-sm-4 grid-listing" data-details="ADCB032B0F1547BEABE4EF3AA78E558F" data-visible="False">
                            
                            <a class="link" href="javascript:;">
                                <img src="/-/media/Site/Guildhall/images/team-game-projects/tokyotempest_poster-web.jpg?h=360&amp;iar=0&amp;w=280&amp;hash=A693DC88A27DB78C5105DCF7459F2F2A" alt="placeholder-280x360" width="280" height="360">
                                <div class="details">
                                    <div class="overlay"></div>

                                        Tokyo Tempest

                        <div class="grid-listing-details-container" id="ADCB032B0F1547BEABE4EF3AA78E558F">
                            <div class="grid-listing-details">
                                <div class="x" data-details="ADCB032B0F1547BEABE4EF3AA78E558F">x</div>

                                <div class="row">
                                    <div class="name col-xs-12">
                                        Tokyo Tempest
                                    </div>
                                </div>

                                <div class="row">
                                    <div class="modal-information col-xs-12">
                                        <span>
                                            2D Game
                                            |</span>
                                        <span>
                                            Arashi Games
                                        </span>
                                    </div>
                                </div>

                                <div class="row">
                                    <div class="modal-summary col-xs-12">
                                        <p><em>Tokyo Tempest</em> is a top-down shoot-em-up in which the player controls rebellious youth Hikaru and uses his mastery of lightning to revolt against the Yakuzas drone army. Players navigate a procedurally generated world in their battle against the machines, making each playthrough a unique experience.&nbsp; The arcade-style scoring system encourages repeated play and challenges the player to overcome his or her own high score. <em>Tokyo Tempest</em> uses the touch interface of Android devices to deliver crisp, responsive gameplay at the tap of a finger.</p>
<p><em><em><em><em>Tokyo Tempest</em>&nbsp;</em></em></em>is a 2D game that was developed by Cohort 25 team Arashi Games as part of the Team Game Production 1 class and was one of the very first games developed by Cohort 25. &nbsp;</p>
                                    </div>
                                </div>

                                    <div class="cols-xs-12 col-md-6  ">

                                            3D Game
                                            |</span>
                                        <span>
                                            Jurassic Sharks
                                        </span>
                                    </div>

                                <div class="row">
                                    <div class="modal-summary col-xs-12">
                                        <p><em>Velocirapture</em> is a first person multiplayer shooter where players step into the role of Sauri warriors. Two clans compete in lethal gladiatorial combat to determine which is superior. Wield deadly weaponry inspired by the extinction events of the ice age and the volcanic upheaval of meteor impact, and decide the fate of your Sauri clan!</p>
<p><em><em><em><em><em><em>Velocirapture</em></em></em>&nbsp;</em></em></em>is a 3D game that was developed by Cohort 25 team Jurassic Sharks and was one of the first 3D games developed by Cohort 25. <em><em>&nbsp;</em></em></p>
